25000,1,"Mix apricot nectar and sugar with buttermilk.  Chill well before serving.  Serving size: 1 cup."
25001,1,"Mix cocoa and sugar.  Add boiling water.  Boil gently 5 minutes.  Mix dry milk with lukewarm water. Stir into cocoa mixture.  Heat to serving temperature.  Serving size:  about 1 cup."
25002,1,"Mix fruit juices and lemonade with water.  Chill thoroughly.  Add ginger ale just before serving.  Serve over ice cubes or crushed ice.  Serving size:  about 1/2 cup without ice."
25003,1,"Heat cider/juice to simmering.  Tie spices in cloth bag or cheese cloth.  Simmer spices with cider /juice 15 minutes. Remove spices.  Serve hot.  Serving size:  3/4 cup."
25004,1,"Combine juices and heat to simmering.  Tie spices in cloth bag or cheese cloth.  Simmer spices with cider 15 minutes.  Remove spices.  Serve hot.  Serving size: 3/4 cup."
25005,1,"Beat sherbet and lemon juice together.  Add honey; mix.  Mix dry milk with skim milk.  Gradually beat milk mixture into sherbet mixture.  Serve immediately in chilled glasses.  Serving size: 1 cup."
25006,1,"Partially thaw strawberries.  Beat strawberries in mixer until well broken up.  Add ice cream.  Beat until well mixed.  In separate bowl, mix dry milk, sugar, and cold skim milk.  Stir milk mixture slowly into ice cream mixture.  Mix well.  Pour into"
25006,2,"chilled glasses.  Serve immediately.  Serving size:  1 cup."
25007,1,"For 100 servings:  beat sugar and shortening until creamy; beat in eggs.  Mix flour, baking powder, baking soda, and salt.  Add dry ingredients, milk, and bananas to creamy mixture; mix only until smooth.  Pour batter into 5 greased loaf pans (about"
25007,2,"9''x5'') about 3 1/2 cups or 1 pound 11 ounces per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F 40 minutes or until batter no longer clings to toothpick inserted in center.  Cool thoroughly.  Slice each loaf into 20 slices.  Serving size: 1 slice."
25008,1,"Mix flour, baking powder, and salt.  Mix in shortening only until mixture is crumbly.  Add enough milk to flour mixture to make a soft dough.  Turn out on lightly floured surface.  Divide dough in half and knead each half lightly about 1 minute.  Roll"
25008,2,"dough out to 1/2 inch thickness.  Cut with a floured 2-inch cutter and place on baking sheets.  Bake at 425 degrees F for 20 minutes or until lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 biscuit.

25009,1,"For 100 servings:  cook celery and onions in margarine until tender; remove from heat.  Stir in bread cubes, seasonings, and broth; toss to mix.  Place in 2 greased baking pans (about 12 by 20 inches), about 1 gallon 1 1/2 quarts or 7 pounds per pan."
25009,2," Cover pans and bake for 30 minutes at 350 degrees F.  Remove cover and bake 30 minutes more or until brown.  Serving size:  1/3 cup."
25010,1,"For 100 servings:  beat sugar, fat, and eggs until creamy.  Mix in milk.  Mix 4 lb 7 oz flour, baking powder and salt.  Add to creamy mixture.  Stir until smooth.  Pour half the batter into 4 greased baking pans (about 12 by 20 inches), about 3 1/2 cups"
25010,2,"or 1 pound 10 ounces per pan.  Mix brown sugar,4 1/2 oz  flour, margarine, and cinnamon.  Sprinkle half the brown sugar mixture over batter in pans, about 3/4 cup or 5 1/4 ounces per pan. Add remaining batter, about 3 1/2 cups or 1 pound 10 ounces per"
25010,3,"pan.  Sprinkle with remaining brown sugar mixture, about 3/4 cup or 5 1/4 ounces per pan.  Bake at 375 degrees F for 20 minutes or until cake springs back when touched lightly.  Serve warm.  Serving size:  1 piece, about 2''x3-3/4''."
25011,1,"For 100 servings:  mix flour, cornmeal, baking powder, sugar, and salt thoroughly.  Mix eggs, milk, and oil.  Add to dry ingredients, stirring only until dry ingredients are moistened; batter will be lumpy.  Pour into 2 greased baking pans (about 12 by 20"
25011,2,"inches), about 2 1/2 quarts or 5 pounds 11 ounces batter per pan.  Bake at 425 degrees F for 25 to 30 minutes or until lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 piece, about 2''x2''."
25012,1,"Add 1/3 cup salt to 6 gallons of boiling water.  Slowly stir in pasta.  Cook until tender-firm, about 8 minutes for macaroni, 6 minutes for noodles, and 10 minutes for spaghetti.  Drain.  Serving size:   about 1/2 cup."
25013,1,"For 100 servings:  pour milk over rolled oats.  Let stand 5 minutes.  Mix in shortening and molasses.  Mix 1 lb 2 oz  flour with salt and yeast.  Add rolled oats mixture and eggs to flour mixture.  Beat well.  Add 1lb 2 oz more flour.  Beat well.  Mix and"
25013,2,"knead in remaining flour.  Place dough in lightly greased bowl and turn once to grease upper side of dough.  Cover and let rise in a warm place until double in size.  Punch down dough to remove air bubbles.  Shape into rolls (about 1-1/2 oz each).  Place"
25013,3,"on sheet pans.  Let rolls rise until double in size.  Bake at 400 degrees F for 16 to 18 minutes or until lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 roll."
25014,1,"For 100 servings:  mix flour, baking powder, sugar, and salt thoroughly.  Mix eggs, oil, and milk.  Add to flour mixture, stirring until dry ingredients are moistened; batter will be lumpy.  Using a No. 24 scoop (2-2/3 T), portion into greased muffin"
25014,2,"tins.  Bake at 400 degrees F for 20 to 25 minutes or lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 muffin."
25015,1,"For 100 servings:  mix flour, baking powder, sugar, and salt thoroughly.  Mix eggs, oil, and milk.  Add to flour mixture, stirring until dry ingredients are moistened; batter will be lumpy.  Gently fold blueberries into the batter.  Using a No. 24 scoop"
25015,2,"(2 2/3 tablespoons) portion into greased muffin tins.  Bake at 400 degrees F for 20 to 25 minutes or until lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 muffin."
25016,1,"For 100 servings:  place rice in 2 baking pans (about 12 by 20 inches), 3 pounds or about 1 quart 3 1/3 cups per pan.  Add salt to boiling water; pour over rice, 3 quarts per pan.  Cover pans tightly.  Bake at 350 degrees F or steam at 5 pounds pressure"
25016,2,"for 25 minutes for white rice and 50 minutes for brown rice.  Remove from oven or steamer and let stand covered 5 minutes.  Serving size:  about 1/2 cup."
25017,1,"For 100 servings:  drain and chop mushrooms; save liquid.  Cook mushrooms, almonds, and onions in margarine until lightly browned.  Add cheese, rice, and parsley.  Mix gently.  Place mixture in 4 baking pans (about 12 by 20 inches), about 2 quarts or 2"
25017,2,"pounds 8 ounces per pan.  Boil 1 3/4 gal mushroom liquid and water.   Stir pepper, basil, and broth into boiling liquid.  Return to boiling.  Pour liquid over rice mixture, about 2 quarts per pan.  Cover; bake at 350 degrees F for 35 minutes.  Serving"
25017,3,"size:  about 1/2 cup."
25018,1,"For 100 servings:  stir in cornmeal and salt into milk.  Cook over low heat, stirring constantly, until thickened to consistency of mush.  Remove from heat.  Stir in margarine.  Cool slightly to about 105 to 110 degrees F.  Stir egg yolks into cornmeal"
25018,2,"mixture.  Mix well.  Beat egg whites until stiff but not dry.  Fold into cornmeal-egg yolk mixture.  Pour into 2 greased baking pans (about 12 by 20 inches), about 1 gallon 1 1/4 quarts or 9 pounds per pan.  Bake at 375 degrees F for 45 minutes or until"
25018,3,"set.  Serving size:  1/3 cup."
25019,1,"For 100 servings:  mix 2 quarts  flour with sugar, yeast, and salt.  Heat milk and oil until warm, stir into flour mixture.  Add eggs; beat well.  Mix in 2 quarts flour, making a soft dough that leaves sides of bowl.  Knead until dough is smooth and"
25019,2,"elastic.  (Kneading may be done in mixing machine.) Place dough in lightly greased bowl and turn over once to grease upper side of dough.  Cover and let rise in warm place until double in size, about 1-1/2 hours.  Punch down dough to remove air bubbles."
25019,3," Shape into rolls about 1-1/4 oz each.  Place rolls on sheet pans.  Let rise until double in size, about 1 hour.  Bake at 400 degrees F for 15 minutes or until lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 roll."
25020,1,"For 100 servings:  mix flours together, and then mix 2 quarts flour with sugar, yeast, and salt.  Heat milk and oil until warm.  Stir into flour mixture.  Add eggs; beat well.  Mix in remaining flour, making a soft dough that leaves the sides of the bowl."
25020,2," Knead until dough is smooth and elastic.  (Kneading may be done in mixing machine.)  Place dough in lightly greased bowl and turn over once to grease upper side of dough.  Cover and let rise in warm place until double in size, about 1-1/2 hours.  Punch"
25020,3,"down dough to remove air bubbles.  Shape into rolls about 1-1/4 oz each.  Place rolls on sheet pans.  Let rise until double in size, about 1 hour.  Bake at 400 degrees F for 15 minutes, or until lightly browned.  Serving size:  1 roll."
25021,1,"For 100 servings:  for pastry, mix flour and salt.  Mix in margarine until size of small peas.  Add 1 cup cold water and mix just until dry ingredients are moistened.  Roll out 4 rectangles (about 12''x20'') on a lightly floured surface, using about 1 lb"
25021,2,"dough for each crust.  For filling, drain apples; save liquid. Place apples in 4 pans (12''x20''), about 3 quarts or 5 lb 12 ounces per pan.  Heat 2 quarts apple liquid and water to boiling.  Add sugar and spices.  Mix cornstarch with remaining liquid."
25021,3," Gradually stir into boiling liquid.  Cook, stirring constantly, until thickened.  Pour thickened mixture over apples, about 4-3/4 c or 2 lb 10 ounces per pan.  Cover apples with pastry.  Cut slits in pastry.  Bake at 425 degrees F for 40 minutes or until"
25021,4,"pastry is brown and filling is bubbly.  Serving size:  1 piece, about 2''x3-3/4''."
25022,1,"Mix sugar, salt, and eggs.  Stir in milk and vanilla.  Pour into 4 baking pans (12''x20''), about 3-1/4 qt or 7 lb per pan.  Sprinkle with nutmeg.  Bake at 350 degrees F for 20 to 25 minutes or until set.  Serving size:  1/2 cup."
25023,1,"Mix tapioca, sugar, salt, and cloves.  Stir in juices.  Cook, stirring constantly, until mixture comes to a boil.  Remove from heat.  Cool, stirring occasionally.  Fold pears into tapioca mixture.  Chill thoroughly.  Serving size:  1/2 cup."
25024,1,"For 100 servings:  add sugar and salt to 1-1/2 gal water.  Heat to simmering.  Beat eggs; mix in 3 qt water.  Stir mixture slowly into cornstarch.  Mix well.  Add egg-cornstarch mixture slowly to heated mixture, stirring constantly.  Continue to stir"
25024,2,"until mixture reaches boiling.  Remove from heat.  Stir in juice, rind, and margarine.  Cool slightly, stirring occasionally.  Chill thoroughly.   Serving size:  1/2 cup."
25025,1,"Cream shortening and sugar until light and fluffy.  Beat in molasses and  eggs.  Mix flour, salt, soda, and ginger.  Add flour mixture and skim milk alternately to shortening mixture.  Stir in oats and dates.  Using a No. 60 scoop (3-1/4 t), drop dough"
25025,2,"onto greased baking sheets.  Bake at 375 degrees F for 15 minutes or until done.  Serving size:  1 cookie."
25026,1,"For 100 servings:  place peaches in 4 pans (12''x20''), about 3 qt or 6 lb 4 oz per pan.  Mix sugar, flour, oats, spices, and fat until crumbly.  Spread evenly over peaches, about 1-1/4 qt or 1 lb 14 oz per pan.  Bake at 375 degrees F for 30 minutes or"
25026,2,"until topping is lightly browned.  Serving size:  1/2 cup."
25027,1,"For 100 servings:  mix crumbs and allspice.  Stir in margarine; mix well.  Press crumb mixture in bottom of 2 baking pans (12''x20''), about 1 qt or 1 lb per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F for 10 minutes or until crumbs are lightly browned.  Drain peaches;"
25027,2,"save 1 1/2 quarts juice.  Coarsely chop peaches. Mix gelatin and sugar.  Add peach liquid.  Heat, stirring constantly, until gelatin is dissolved.  Stir in orange juice concentrate, almond extract, and vanilla.  Chill until mixture is consistency of egg"
25027,3,"whites.  Whip until light and fluffy.  Stir in yogurt and peaches.  Pour filling into baked crust, about 1-1/4 gal or 7 lb per pan.  Chill until firm.  Serving size:  1 piece, about 2''x2''."
25028,1,"For 100 servings:  for crust, mix flour and salt.  Mix in margarine until size of small peas.  Add water and mix just until dry ingredients are moistened.  Roll out 12 crusts on lightly floured surface, using about 8 oz dough for each crust.  Line 12 pie"
25028,2,"pans, about 9 inches in diameter, with pastry.  For filling, add pumpkin to milk; heat until bubbles appear.  Mix sugars, flour, salt, and spices.  Add eggs; mix well.  Stir egg mixture into hot pumpkin mixture.  Fill pie crusts with mixture using 3-3/4 c"
25028,3,"or 2 lb per pan.  Bake at 375 degrees F for 40 minutes or until filling is set.  Serving size:  1/8 pie.  Makes 12 pies.  Serving size:  1/8 pie."

25029,2,"bread and raisins.  Bake at 325 degrees F for 45 minutes or until set.  Serving size:  1 piece, 2''x2''."

25030,2,"18''x26'' or 2 cakes, 12''x20''.  Serving size:  about 1-1/3 T."

25031,2,"mixture returns to simmering.  Remove from heat.  Cool quickly, stirring occasionally.  Chill.  Serving size:  about 1/2 cup."
25032,1,"For 100 servings:  mix sugar, salt, and chocolate with 2-1/2 gal milk.  Heat to simmering.  Beat eggs; mix with 2 qt milk and vanilla.  Stir slowly into cornstarch. Mix until smooth.  Stir egg mixture slowly into hot milk mixture.  Cook, stirring"
25032,2,"constantly, until mixture returns to simmering.  Remove from heat.  Cool quickly, stirring occasionally.  Chill.  Serving size:  about 1/2 cup."

25035,1,"For 100 servings:  break eggs into small bowl.  Any shell fragments in bowl should be removed.  Pour broken out eggs into mixer bowl.  When all eggs are in mixer bowl, beat slightly to break yolks.  Add milk and salt.  Beat until well mixed.  Place 2 T"
25035,2,"margarine in each of two baking pans (12''x20'').  Pour egg mixture into pans, about 3 qt or 6 lb 6 oz per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F until eggs are well done and dry, about 25 minutes, stirring after 15 minutes and again after 20 minutes.  Stir to break"
25035,3,"up chunks.  Serve with Number 16 scoop (1/4 c).  Serving size:  1/4 cup or 1 egg."
25036,1,"For 100 servings:  sort beans; wash, if needed.  Add beans to 3 gallons boiling water.  Boil 2 minutes.  Remove from heat.  Cover and let soak 1 hour or if more convenient, cool and let stand overnight in refrigerator.  Add 1/2 t salt for each lb of dry"
25036,2,"beans.  Cook in soaking liquid until tender (1/2 hour).  Add boiling water, if needed.  Drain; serve or use in recipe.  Serving size:  3 ounces."

25037,2,"beans.  Cook in soaking liquid until tender (1 to 1-1/2 hours).  Add boiling water, if needed.  Drain; serve or use in recipe.  Serving size:  3 ounces."

25046,1,"For 100 servings:  bring sufficient water to boil in heavy stockpot or steam-jacketed kettle to cover eggs.  Cook in batches of 50 eggs for ease in handling.  Gently lower eggs into water, using perforated basket or large slotted spoon.  Return to water"
25046,2,"to simmering.  Simmer 20 minutes.  Remove eggs from stockpot or kettle.  Plunge into cold water.  To serve warm, remove eggs immediately from cold water.  Or, to serve cold or use in salads, hold eggs in cold water until eggs are cool, about 10 minutes."
25046,3," Change water if necessary to keep it cold.  Refrigerate.  To crack and shell eggs, roll eggs gently to break shell.  Start peeling from large end.  Serve.  Serving size:  1 egg."
25047,1,"For 100 servings:  trim fat from roasts.  Place roasts on racks in shallow open roasting pans.  Allow space in pans between roasts.  Insert a meat thermometer into the center of the smallest roast so the tip is not touching bone, fat, or gristle.  Roast"
25047,2,"at 325 degrees F until the thermometer reads 160 degrees F (3-1/4 TO 4-1/2 hours).  Remove roast from pan.  Move thermometer to the next larger roast; follow this procedure until all the meat is cooked.  Let roasts stand 15 to 20 minutes; then slice and"
25047,3,"serve immediately to insure highest quality.  Serving size:  3 ounces."

25058,1,"For 100 servings:  trim fat from roasts.  Place roasts on racks in shallow open roasting pans.  Allow space in pans between roasts.  Insert a meat thermometer into the center of the smallest roast so the tip is not touching bone, fat, or gristle.  Roast"
25058,2,"at 325 degrees F until the thermometer reads 140 degrees F (approximate roasting time = 1-1/2 to 2-1/2 hr).  Remove roast from pan.  Move thermometer to the next larger roast; follow this procedure until all the meat is cooked.  Let roasts stand 15 to 20"
25058,3,"minutes; then slice and serve immediately to insure highest quality.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25059,1,"For 100 servings:  trim fat from roasts.  Place roasts on racks in shallow open roasting pans.  Allow space in pans between roasts.  Insert a meat thermometer into the center of the smallest roast so the tip is not touching bone, fat, or gristle.  Roast"
25059,2,"at 325 degrees F until the thermometer reads 170 degrees F (approximate roasting time 2 to 3 hr).  Remove roast from pan.  Move thermometer to the next larger roast; follow this procedure until all the meat is cooked.  Let roasts stand 15 to 20 minutes;"
25059,3,"then slice and serve immediately to insure highest quality.  Serving size:  3 ounces."

25061,2,"hours).  Remove roasts from pan and let stand 15 to 20 minutes; slice and serve.  Serving size:  3 oz lean meat."

25075,1,"For 100 servings:  brown meat in a kettle, pot, or tilting skillet, and cover with water.  Cover; bring to simmering.  Simmer until fork tender (3 - 4 hours).  Remove from pot.  Let large pieces stand 20 minutes; slice and serve.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25076,1,"For 100 servings:  brown meat in a kettle, pot, or tilting skillet, and cover with water.  Cover; bring to simmering.  Simmer until fork tender (3 - 4 hours).  Remove from pot.  Let large pieces stand 20 minutes; slice and serve.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25077,1,"For 100 servings:  thaw and clean turkey.  Fold the neck skin over to the back and fasten with a skewer.  Tie legs together over the body opening or if there is a band of skin above the tail, tuck legs into it.  Place whole turkeys in shallow pans."
25077,2," Insert thermometer in whole turkeys so the thermometer is in the center of the inner thigh muscle toward the body.  Insert thermometer into the center of the thickest part of the breast or thigh pieces.  Be sure the thermometer does not touch bone."
25077,3," Roast at 325 degrees F until thermometer registers 185 degrees F (3-1/2 to 7-1/2 hours, depending upon the size of the whole turkeys)."
25078,1,"For 100 servings:  thaw and clean chicken.  Put in stock pot or steam-jacketed kettle.  Add enough hot water to barely cover chicken.  Season with vegetables or herbs if desired.  Cover and simmer until tender (1 to 4 hours, depending upon the size of the"
25078,2,"chickens).  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25079,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Cook at 350 degrees F for 30 to 40 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25080,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Cook at 425 degrees F for 30 to 40 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25081,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Cook at 400 degrees F for 15 to 20 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25082,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Broil for 10 to 15 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25083,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Simmer for 5 to 10 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25084,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Steam for 5 to 10 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25085,1,"Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque and flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Steam for 10 to 15 minutes.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces."
25086,1,"Steam for 15 to 20 minutes.  Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  4-1/2 ounces cooked meat per lobster."
25087,1,"Steam for 3 to 5 minutes.  Cook only until fish flesh becomes opaque.  Do not overcook.  Serving size:  3 ounces of cooked shrimp meat."
25088,1,"For 100 servings:  sort and wash beans.  Add beans to boiling water.  Return to boiling.  Boil 2 minutes.  Remove from heat; cover.  Soak 1 hour or place in refrigerator overnight.  Add 2 Tbsp salt to beans.  Cover and cook gently until beans are tender,"
25088,2,"about 1-1/2 hours.  Drain; save 1-3/4 gallons bean liquid.  Place cooked, drained beans in 4 pans (12''x20''), about 1-1/4 gal or 8 lb per pan.  Mix remaining ingredients.  Pour over beans in pans, about 3 qt or 6 lb 8 oz per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F"
25088,3,"for 2 hours; stir after 1 hour.  Stir again, if needed, to prevent drying.  Serving size:  3/4 cup."
25089,1,"For 100 servings:  thaw fillets and divide into 100 servings, about 4 oz each.  Place in a single layer, skin side down on 4 greased sheet pans (18''x26''), 25 servings per pan.  Mix margarine, lemon juice, lemon rind, salt, and pepper.  Pour mixture over"
25089,2,"fish about 1 c or 3 oz per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F for 25 to 30 minutes or until fish flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Serving size:  1 piece."
25090,1,"For 100 servings:  cook macaroni in 6 gal boiling water until tender, about 12 minutes.  Drain.  Place in 4 baking pans (12''x20''), about 2-3/4 qt or 4 lb per pan.  Melt margarine; stir in flour, mustard, and salt.  Gradually stir in milk.  Cook,"
25090,2,"stirring constantly, until thickened.  Add cheese; stir until cheese melts.  Pour sauce over cooked macaroni, about 2-1/2 qt or 5 lb 10 oz per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F for 35-40 minutes until lightly browned.  Serving size:  2/3 cup."
25091,1,"For 100 servings:  thaw frozen fish fillets.  Cook onions and celery in margarine until tender.  Stir in bread cubes, parsley, seasonings, and milk; toss to mix.  Arrange half the fillets in 4 greased pans (12''x20''), about 3 lb per pan.  Spread bread"
25091,2,"cube mixture over fillets, using about 1 gal or 2 lb 4 oz per pan.  Arrange remaining fillets over bread cube mixture, about 3 lb per pan.  Brush fillets with 1 c melted margarine.  Cover pans and bake at 325 degrees F for 40 minutes.  Mix 1/2 c margarine"
25091,3,"with parsley.  Uncover fillets and brush with margarine mixture.  Return to oven and bake uncovered an additional 10 minutes or until fish flakes easily when tested with a fork.  Serving size:  1 piece, 2''x3-3/4''."
25092,1,"For 100 servings:  trim fat from beef cubes.  Brown cubes well.  Drain off fat.  Add water and salt.  Cover; cook until beef is tender, about 2 hours.  Add onions and carrots to beef; cook 5 minutes.  Add peas, cook 5 minutes longer.  Mix flour, pepper,"
25092,2,"and water until smooth.  Gently stir into meat and vegetable mixture.  Cook, stirring constantly, until thickened.  Pour mixture into 4 baking pans (12''x20''), about 1 gal or 8 lb 8 oz per pan.  Boil potatoes until tender.  Drain.  Mash potatoes in mixer"
25092,3,"until smooth.  Add salt and margarine.  Gradually add enough milk to moisten.  Beat on high speed until potatoes are light and fluffy.  Spread mashed potatoes on beef mixture in pans, about 2 qt or 3 lb 7-1/2 oz per pan.  Sprinkle potatoes with paprika."
25092,4," Bake at 400 degrees F for 30 minutes or until potatoes are lightly browned.  Serving size:  2/3 c beef mixture, 1/3 c potatoes."
25093,1,"For 100 servings:  wash chicken.  Drain.  Place chicken pieces in 6 baking pans (12''x20''), 16 to 17 pieces per pan.  Bake at 400 degrees F until chicken is brown, about 1 hour.  Cook onions in boiling water until tender.  Stir in remaining ingredients."
25093,2," Bring to boiling.  Cook 10 minutes to blend flavors.  Pour tomato mixture over chicken pieces, about 1-1/2 qt or 3 lb 4 oz per pan.  Return to oven and bake 20 to 25 minutes or until chicken is tender.  Serving size:  1 breast half or leg and 1/3 c"
25093,3,"sauce."
25094,1,"For 100 servings:  cook onions, green peppers, and celery in 1 1/3 cups (10 1/2 oz) margarine until tender.  Stir in flour, salt, and pepper.  Gradually stir in chicken broth.  Cook, stirring constantly, until thickened.  Mix hot mixture with corn,"
25094,2,"chicken, and cheese.  Pour into 4 baking pans (12''x20''), about 3-1/2 qt or 7 lb 12 oz per pan.  Mix breadcrumbs with 1/2 cup (4 oz) melted margarine.  Sprinkle evenly over mixture in pans, about 2-3/4 oz per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F for 45 minutes or"
25094,3,"until bubbly and crumbs are lightly browned.  Serving size:  1/2 c   Variation:  Use turkey broth and cooked turkey in place of chicken broth and cooked chicken."

25095,2,"and eggs.  Mix well.  Spread mixture evenly into 2 greased baking pans (12''x20''), about 4-1/2 qt or 9 lb 14 oz per pan.  Bake at 350 degrees F for 45 minutes or until done in the center.  Serving size:  1 piece, 2''x2''."

25125,1,"For 100 servings:  drain grapefruit and orange sections.  Save 1 gal liquid.  Soften gelatin in 1 qt fruit liquid.  Add sugar; stir into boiling water.  Stir until gelatin and sugar are dissolved.  Add lemon juice and 3 qt fruit liquid.  Chill until"
25125,2,"mixture begins to thicken.  Mix in grapefruit and orange sections and cherries.  Pour into 4 pans (12''x20''), about 3-1/2 qt or 7 lb 11 oz per pan.  Chill until set.  Cut and serve on lettuce leaves.  Serving size:  1 piece, 2''x3-3/4''."
25126,1,"For 100 servings:  soften gelatin in cold water.  Stir into boiling water.  Stir until gelatin is dissolved.  Stir in salt, sugar, and lemon juice.  Chill until mixture begins to thicken.  Stir vegetables into gelatin mixture.  Pour into 4 pans"

25187,1,"For best results, have all ingredients and utensils at room temperature.  Dissolve dry yeast in warm water.  Let stand 4-5 minutes.  Place all dry ingredients (flours, dry milk, sugar, and salt) in mixer bowl.  Using a dough hook, blend on low speed"
25187,2,"approximately 2 minutes.  Add oil and blend on low speed for approximately 2 minutes.  Add water.  Mix on low speed for 1 minute.  Add dissolved yeast and mix on low speed for 2 minutes.  Knead dough on medium speed for 8 minutes, or until dough is smooth"
25187,3,"and elastic.  Place dough in warm area (about 90 degrees F) for 45-60 minutes.  Punch down dough to remove air bubbles.  Form rolls from dough by pinching off 2 oz pieces and shaping.  Place rolls on 2 lightly oiled sheet pans (18''x26''x1'') in rows of"
25187,4,"10 down and 5 across.  Place in a warm area (about 90 degrees F) until double in size, 30-50 minutes.  Bake in a conventional oven until lightly browned, at 400 degrees F for 18-20 minutes.  Brush lightly with melted butter or margarine (approximately 1"
25187,5,"Tbsp per pan) while warm."
25188,1,"Heat oil.  Add onions and green pepper.  Cook for 5 minutes.  Add water, tomatoes, tomato paste, and seasonings.  Bring to boil.  Stir in rice.  Return to boil.  Reduce heat and cover tightly.  Cook over low heat for 20-30 minutes or until rice is tender."
25188,2," Pour into serving pans.  Portion with No. 16 scoop (1/4 c). "
25189,1,"Mash drained sweet potatoes.  Set aside.  Blend flour, sugar, dry milk, baking powder, baking soda, salt, allspice, nutmeg, and cloves for 1 minute in mixer on low speed.  Combine eggs and water.  Add shortening and liquid mixture to dry ingredients."
25189,2," Blend for 1 minute on low speed.  Beat for 1 minute on medium speed.  Add mashed sweet potatoes, prunes and nuts.  Blend for 30 seconds on low speed.  Beat for 1 minute on medium speed.  Do not over mix.  Batter will be lumpy.  Pour 6 lb 14 oz (3-1/4 qt)"
25189,3,"batter in each of 2 steamtable pans (12''x20''x2-1/2'') which has been lightly greased.  Bake in a conventional oven at 350 degrees F for 55-65 minutes.  Cool.  Cut each pan 5x10 (50 pieces per pan)."

25190,2,"hook, blend on low speed for approximately 2 minutes.  Add 1 quart water and mix on low speed for 1 minute.  Add dissolved yeast and mix on low speed for 2 minutes.  Add shortening  and mix on low speed for 2 minutes.  Knead dough on medium speed for 8"
25190,3,"minutes, or until dough is smooth and elastic.  Place dough in a warm area (about 90 degrees F)  for 45-60 minutes.  Divide dough into 4 pieces, 1 lb 15 oz each.  Shape each piece into a loaf and place in a loaf pan (16-1/2''x4-1/2''x4''), which has been"

25196,1,"For 100 servings:  for pastry topping: Combine flour and salt.  Mix in shortening until size of small peas.  Add water and mix just until dry ingredients are moistened.  Cover and set aside.  For filling:  Drain apples, reserving juice.  Set aside.  Add"
25196,2,"enough water to apple juice to make 1 gal liquid mixture.  Mix cornstarch with about 1/4 of the liquid mixture.  Bring remaining liquid mixture to boil.  Add about 1/2 of the sugar.  Gradually add cornstarch mixture to boiling liquid.  Cook, stirring"
25196,3,"constantly, until thickened.  Mixture will be very thick, but will thin after other steps.  Remove from heat.  Blend remaining sugar, cinnamon, and nutmeg thoroughly into mixture.  Add apples to thickened mixture.  Stir lightly.  Do not break up fruit."
25196,4," Pour 3-3/4 qt thickened apple mixture into each of 4 steam table pans (12''x20''x2-1/2'').  Roll out pastry dough into rectangles (about 12''x20'') on lightly floured surface.  Use about 1 lb dough for each pan.  Cover apples with pastry.  Brush with"
25196,5,"pastry brush dipped in water.  Cut slits in pastry.  Bake in a conventional oven at 425 degrees F for 1 hour.  Cut each pan 5x5 (25 portions per pan)."

25208,2,"and salt until blended.  With spoon, stir in oats.  Spray 2 large cookie sheets with nonstick cooking spray.  Spoon dough by level 1/3 cup measures onto cookie sheets, about 3 inches apart.   With floured hands, roll dough in balls.  Bake cookies 12 to 15"
25208,3,"minutes until golden; remove to wire racks to cool.  Store cookies in tightly covered container.  Makes about 15 jumbo-size cookies.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping."

25216,1,"For 100 servings: for bottom crust:  Combine 3 qt 1/2 cup flour and 1 Tbsp salt.  Mix in shortening until size of small peas.  Add 2 1/2 cups water and mix just until dry ingredients are moistened.  Roll out pastry dough into rectangles (20''x28'') on"
25216,2,"lightly floured surface.  Use 3 lb 5 oz dough for each crust.  Line bottom and sides of 2 sheet pans (18''x26''x1'') with dough.  For pie filling:  Puree or mash drained sweet potatoes until very smooth and free of lumps. (Discard coarse fibers that stick"
25216,3,"to beater blades.)   Add beaten eggs, milk, margarine, brown sugar, salt, flour, lemon juice, cinnamon, ginger, and cloves.  Beat for 4 minutes on medium speed until smooth and well blended.  Pour 9 lb 2 oz (1 gal) pie filling into each crust.  Bake until"
25216,4,"a knife inserted near the center comes out clean.  Bake in a conventional oven at 425 degrees F for 15 minutes, then reduce the oven temperature to 375 degrees F for 45-55 minutes.  Cool.  Cut each pan 5x10 (50 pieces per pan).  For whipped topping:"
25216,5," Soften gelatin in 1/2 cup cold water.  Combine dry milk and water.  Whip until free of lumps.  Heat to scalding.  Remove from heat.  Add softened gelatin and stir until dissolved.  Cover.  Refrigerate overnight.  (Chilling overnight produces a thicker"
25216,6,"mixture.)  Whip chilled mixture in mixer for 10 minutes on high speed.  Add sugar, salt, and vanilla.  Beat for 5 minutes on high speed until very stiff.  Use immediately or keep chilled until service.  Top each piece of pie with 2 T whipped topping."
25217,1,"Cream margarine and shortening in mixer at medium speed for 2 minutes until light and fluffy.  Combine powdered sugar, salt, and dry milk.  Add to creamed margarine.  Mix for 1 minute on low speed.  Add vanilla while mixing at low speed.  Slowly add water"
25217,2,"to obtain a spreading consistency.  Scrape down bowl.  Beat at medium speed for 5 minutes or until mixture is creamy and well blended.  (For a thinner frosting, add additional water, 1 tsp at a time, mixing after each addition.)  Spread on cooled cakes."
25217,3," One serving = 1-1/4 T."

25286,1,"For 100 servings:  for best results, have all ingredients and utensils at room temperature.  Dissolve dry yeast in warm water.  Let stand for 4-5 minutes.  Place flour in mixer bowl.  Make well in the center.  Pour in dissolved yeast, oil, salt, and"
25286,2,"sugar.  Gradually work into the flour using dough hook on low speed.  Knead for 15 minutes on medium speed.  Divide and shape dough into 5 balls, 1 lb 12 oz each.  Let rest for 20 minutes.  Combine seasonings in small bowl.  On lightly floured surface,"
25286,3,"roll out each ball of dough into a rectangle 16'' wide and 24'' long.  Layer ingredients lengthwise along the center of the dough rectangle as follows.  Leave 6'' border across the top and bottom of dough for folding over later.  1st layer - 10 oz cheese."
25286,4," 2nd layer - approximately 1/2 tsp seasoning mix.  3rd layer - 14-1/2 oz turkey ham slices.  Fold top third of dough over cheese and turkey ham.  Place another layer of cheese, seasonings, and turkey ham on top of folded dough as follows:  1st layer - 10"
25286,5,"oz cheese.  2nd layer - approximately 1/2 tsp seasoning mix.  3rd layer - 14-1/2 oz turkey ham.  Fold bottom third of dough over the second layer of cheese and turkey ham.  Pinch to seal end and top seams.  (If desired, brush seams with egg wash.)  Using"
25286,6,"a fork, pierce top of dough lengthwise from end to end, repeating 4 rows across.  Place rolled dough on lightly oiled sheet pan (18''x26''x1'').  Two strombolis can be placed on each sheet pan.  Allow rolled stromboli to rise for 30 minutes.  Bake until"
25286,7,"crust is lightly browned.  Bake in a conventional oven at 400 degrees F for 30-35 minutes.  Remove from oven.  Let stand for 15 minutes before cutting, to prevent cheese from running.  Cut each stromboli lengthwise down the middle and crosswise 10 times"
25286,8,"into 20 portions.  Makes 5 stromboli rolls, 20 pieces each."

28503,1,"Line large cookie sheet with foil.  Using 10 inch round plate as a guide, with a toothpick, outline a circle on foil on cookie sheet.  In small bowl, with mixer at high speed, beat egg whites, salt, and cream of tartar until soft peaks form.  Beating at"
28503,2,"high speed, gradually sprinkle in sugar, 2 tablespoons at a time,  beating well after each addition until sugar dissolves and whites stand in stiff, glossy peaks.  Preheat oven to 200F.  Spread half of meringue inside circle to form a 1/4 inch thick"
28503,3,"base.  Spoon remaining meringue onto edge of base to form a 1 1/2 inch high border.  Bake 3 1/2 hours or until meringue is crisp but not brown.  Turn oven off and let meringue cool in oven 30 minutes.  Remove from oven; cool completely on cookie sheet on"
28503,4,"rack.  When meringue is cool, carefully loosen and remove meringue from foil and place on serving plate.  Thinly slice 1 1/2 bananas; arrange over bottom of meringue shell.  In large bowl, prepare instant pudding as label directs but use only 1 cup"
28503,5,"low-fat milk.  With rubber spatula, gently fold whipped topping into pudding.  Spread filling over bananas in meringue shell.  In small saucepan over low heat, heat apple jelly until melted; remove from heat and cool slightly.  Cut remaining bananas"
28503,6,"diagonally into thin slices.  Arrange banana slices over filling in concentric circles; brush with apple jelly.  Garnish with lemon slice and lemon leaves.  Makes 12 servings.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping. "

28532,2,"mixer at high speed, beat egg whites, cream of tartar, and almond extract until soft peaks form; gradually beat in 1/2 cup, 2 tablespoons at a time, beating well after each addition until sugar completely dissolves and whites stand in stiff peaks.  With"
28532,3,"rubber spatula, gently fold flour mixture into egg mixture.  Spread batter evenly in pan; bake 15 or 20 minutes until top of cake springs back when lightly touched.  Meanwhile, sprinkle clean cloth towel with cocoa.  When cake is done, loosen edges of"
28532,4,"cake from sides of jelly-roll pan.  Immediately invert cake onto towel.  Carefully peel waxed paper from cake.  Starting at a narrow end, roll cake with towel, jelly-roll fashion.  Cool cake completely, seam-side down, on wire rack, about 1 hour.  Remove"
28532,5,"tofu frozen dessert from freezer to counter top to soften slightly.  Unroll  cooled cake; evenly spread half the cake crosswise with one flavor tofu frozen dessert; spread other half of cake with remaining flavor tofu frozen dessert.  Starting from same"
28532,6,"narrow end,  roll cake without towel.  Place rolled cake, seam-side down, on long platter.  Freeze cake until firm, at least 4 hours.  To serve, let cake roll stand at room temperature 15 minutes for easier slicing.  Makes 12 servings.   Recipe provided"

28535,1," In large bowl, combine yeast, sugar,  salt, and 2 1/2 cups all-purpose flour.  In 2 quart saucepan over low heat, heat molasses, 4 tablespoons margarine, and 1 3/4 cups water until mixture is very warm (125 to 130F.).  Margarine or butter does not need"
28535,2,"to melt.  With mixer at low speed, gradually beat liquid into dry ingredients just until blended.  Increase speed to medium; beat 2 minutes, occasionally scraping bowl with rubber spatula.  Beat in oat-flour blend, 1 egg, and 1 egg yolk, to make a thick"
28535,3,"batter; continue beating 2 minutes, scraping bowl often.  Reserve egg white to brush on loaf later.  With wooden spoon, stir in 2 cups all-purpose flour to make a soft dough.  Turn dough onto lightly floured surface and knead until smooth and elastic,"
28535,4,"about 10 minutes, working in more all-purpose flour (about 3/4 cup) while kneading.  Shape dough into ball; cover and let rest 15 minutes for easier shaping.  Grease large cookie sheet.  With floured rolling pin, roll dough into 18'' by 12'' rectangle;"
28535,5,"brush with 2 tablespoons melted margarine.  From on 18 inch side, tightly roll dough jelly-roll fashion; pinch seams to seal.  Place roll, seam-side down, on cookie sheet; tuck ends under to seal.  Cover and let rise in a warm place until doubled, about"
28535,6,"30 minutes.  Preheat oven to 350F.  Cut 5 or 6 diagonal slashes on top of loaf.  In cup, with fork beat remaining egg white.  Brush loaf with egg white; sprinkle with oats.  Bake 40 minutes or until bread sounds hollow when lightly tapped with fingers;"
28535,7,"cover last 10 minutes, if necessary, to prevent over browning.  Remove loaf from cookie sheet to wire rack.  Cool bread slightly to serve warm.  Or, cool completely to serve cold later.  Make 18 servings.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping. "
28536,1," In bowl, stir flour, sugar, and 1/4 teaspoon salt.  With pastry blender or two knives used scissor-fashion, cut in light corn oil spread until mixture resembles coarse crumbs.  Sprinkle 3 to 4 tablespoons cold water, 1 tablespoon at a time, into flour"
28536,2,"mixture, mixing lightly with a fork after each addition, until dough is just moist enough to hold together.  Shape dough into a ball; wrap in plastic wrap and refrigerate 45 minutes or until well chilled.  Meanwhile, prepare filling:  Drain pear halves;"
28536,3,"reserve 5 of the largest pear halves for top of pie.  Spoon remaining pears into 3 quart saucepan; with potato masher or fork, mash pears with brown sugar, cinnamon, and 1/4 teaspoon salt until almost smooth.  Over medium-high heat, heat mashed pear"
28536,4,"mixture to boiling; reduce heat to medium.  Continue cooking pear mixture until all liquid from pears has evaporated and mixture is very thick, stirring frequently, about 25 minutes.  Cool pear mixture until lukewarm.  Preheat oven to 425F.  On floured"
28536,5,"surface, with floured rolling pin, roll dough into a round about 1 inch larger all around than 10 inch tart pan with removable bottom.  Line pan with dough round, pressing onto bottom and up side of pan; trim edge even with top of pan.  Reserve trimmings."
28536,6," With fork, prick bottom and side of dough in tart pan in many places.  Line dough with foil.  Bake crust 15 minutes.  Remove foil; prick again; bake 15 minutes longer or until golden (if crust puffs up during baking, gently press it to pan with spoon)."
28536,7," Meanwhile, reroll trimmings and cut into several leaf-shape pieces.  Bake leaves on small cookie sheet on another rack during last 10 minutes of tart shell baking time.  Cool tart shell in pan and pastry leaves on wire rack.  Pour cooled pear mixture"
28536,8,"into tart shell.  Cut reserved pear halves into thin slices; arrange sliced pears on pear mixture to cover entire top off tart.  In small saucepan over low heat, heat apple jelly until melted.  Brush pears with melted apple jelly.  Garnish tart with"
28536,9,"pastry leaves.  Makes 10 servings.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping. "

28565,1,"In large bowl, combine yeast, salt, 2 cups whole wheat flour and 1 cup all-purpose flour.  In 2 quart saucepan over low heat, heat honey, margarine, and 2 cups water until very warm (125 to 130F.).  Margarine does not need to melt.  With mixer at low"
28565,2,"speed, gradually beat honey mixture into dry ingredients just until blended.  Increase speed to medium; beat 2 minutes, occasionally scraping bowl with rubber spatula.  Beat in 1 egg, 1 egg yolk, and 3/4 cup whole wheat flour to make a thick batter;"
28565,3,"continue beating 2 minutes, scraping bowl often.  Refrigerate egg white to brush on rolls later.  With wooden spoon, stir in wheat germ, 1 cup oats, and 2 1/4 cups all-purpose flour to make a soft dough.  Turn dough onto lightly floured surface and knead"
28565,4,"until smooth and elastic, about 10 minutes, working in more flour (about 3/4 cup) while kneading.  Shape dough into a ball; cover and let rest 15 minutes.  Grease 17'' by 11 1/2'' roasting pan.  Cut dough into 24 equal pieces; shape into balls and place"
28565,5,"in roasting pan.  Cover and let rise until doubled, about 40 minutes.  Preheat oven to 400F.  In cup, with fork, beat reserved egg white.  Brush rolls with egg white; sprinkle with remaining oats.  Bake rolls 15 to 20 minutes until golden and rolls sound"
28565,6,"hollow when lightly tapped.  Serve warm.  Or, cool in pan on rack to serve later.  Reheat if desired.  Pull rolls apart to serve.  Makes 2 dozen rolls.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping. "

28587,2,"dough.  Preheat oven to 400F.  On lightly greased 14 inch round pizza pan, press first ball of dough to edge of dough, leaving 1 inch border; top with chopped broccoli (thawed and squeezed dry), spinach (thawed and squeezed dry), roasted red peppers, and"
28587,3,"sliced tomatoes.  Sprinkle with shredded mozzarella cheese.  On lightly floured surface, with floured rolling pin, roll second ball of dough into a 14 inch round.  Fold round in half and transfer to top of pizza; unfold, and with fork, press edges of"
28587,4,"dough together to seal.  Brush top of pizza with olive oil.  Garnish top with a few fresh rosemary sprigs.  Cut a few short slashes on top to allow steam to escape during baking.  Bake pizza on bottom rack in oven 25 to 30 minutes until crust is golden"
28587,5,"brown and filling is hot.  Makes 12 servings. "

28588,3,"and squeeze spinach.  Stir in ricotta cheese and spinach until blended.  Preheat oven to 375F.  Drain shells.  Fill cooked shells with chicken mixture.  Spoon half of sauce into 13'' by 9'' glass or ceramic baking dish.  Arrange filled shells in sauce."
28588,4," Spoon remaining sauce over shells.  Cover baking dish with foil and bake 40 minutes or until shells are heated through and the sauce is hot and bubbly.  Makes 8 main-dish servings.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping. "
28589,1,"The Summer Salad Duet consists of a Tuna and White Bean Salad, Green Bean and Potato Salad, and Herbed Bread Sticks.  If not serving right away, cover salad and refrigerate; wrap Herbed Bread Sticks with plastic wrap and set aside.  TUNA & WHITE BEAN"
28589,2,"SALAD:  In large bowl, mix the first 5 ingredients; red wine vinegar, Dijon mustard, fresh basil, salt and pepper.  Add next two ingredients, tuna, drained and flaked, and the white kidney beans, drained.  Toss gently to mix well.  GREEN BEAN & POTATO"
28589,3,"SALAD:  Drain potatoes and rinse.  Thaw the green beans under running warm water; drain; pat dry with paper towels.  Slice cherry tomatoes in half.  In large bowl, mix next 4 ingredients; oil, oregano, salt and pepper.  Add potatoes, green beans, cherry"
28589,4,"tomatoes.  Toss gently to mix well.  HERBED BREAD STICKS:  Cut half Italian bread diagonally into 1 inch thick slices.  Cut each slice lengthwise in half.  In cup, mix next 4 ingredients; oil, parsley, salt and pepper.  Brush bread sticks with olive oil"
28589,5,"mixture.  To serve, line 4 dinner plates with lettuce leaves.  Spoon tuna mixture onto lettuce.  Sprinkle top of tuna with red onion slices.  Arrange beets, green bean and potato mixture, and bread sticks on to plates with tuna salad.  Makes 4 main dish"

28590,1,"Cut carrots and celery into 1/4'' thick slices.  Coarsely chop escarole.  In 8 quart Dutch oven or saucepot over medium-high heat, in hot olive oil, cook carrots, celery, and onion, stirring frequently, until vegetables are golden.  Meanwhile, rinse"
28590,2,"chicken with running cold water.  Remove skin and as much fat as possible from chicken.  Into Dutch oven with vegetables, place chicken, breast side down, and 10 cups water; over high heat, heat to boiling.  Reduce heat to low; cover and simmer 30 minutes"
28590,3,"or until chicken is fork-tender.  Remove chicken to bowl; refrigerate until chicken is cool enough to handle.  While chicken is cooling, to vegetable mixture in Dutch oven, add barley, salt, chicken bouillon, and pepper; over high heat, heat to boiling."
28590,4," Reduce heat to low; cover and simmer 1 1/4 hours or until barley is tender.  Discard the bones and any remaining skin and fat from the chicken; tear chicken meat into bite-size pieces.  When barley is tender, stir in chicken, stewed tomatoes, and"
28590,5,"escarole; over high heat, heat to boiling.  Reduce heat to low; cover and simmer 5 minutes to wilt escarole and blend flavors, stirring occasionally.  Skim fat from soup, if any.  Makes 12 servings.   Recipe provided by Good Housekeeping. "

28600,3,"zucchini, mushrooms, salt, oregano, and pepper; cook, stirring occasionally, until vegetables are golden brown and tender-crisp.   Remove skillet from heat.  In 5 quart Dutch oven or saucepot over high heat, in 1 inch boiling water, heat carrots and"
28600,4,"cauliflower to boiling.  Reduce heat to low; cover and simmer 5 minutes.  Stir in artichokes and green beans; over high heat, heat to boiling.  Reduce heat to low; cover and simmer 5 minutes longer or until all vegetables are tender; drain.  Return carrot"
28600,5,"mixture to Dutch oven.  After barley has cooked 1 hour, remove cover and cook over high heat until most of liquid is absorbed.  Drain and rinse black beans.  Stir barley, zucchini mixture, and black beans into carrot mixture in Dutch oven; heat through."

MICROWAVE METHOD

CONVENTIONAL METHOD
1. Preheat oven to 400 F.  Lightly grease a cooking sheet.
2. Place chicken pieces on cooking sheet so they are not touching.
3. Bake until golden brown, about 12 to 14"
33097,3,"minutes.

MICROWAVE METHOD
1. Lightly grease an 8- by 12-inch baking dish.
2. Place chicken pieces on baking dish so they are not touching.  Cover with waxed paper and cook on high.
3. Rotate chicken every 2 to 3 minutes.  Cook until tender, about 6"
33097,4,"to 8 minutes.

Note:  To remove bone from chicken thighs:
1. Place chicken on cutting board.  Remove skin from thighs.
2. Turn chicken thighs over.
3. Cut around bone and remove it."

33104,1,"1. Scrub potatoes and remove any blemishes.

TO BAKE:
CONVENTIONAL METHOD
1. Preheat oven to 400F.
2. Place potatoes in oven and bake until tender, about 30 to 40 minutes.

MICROWAVE METHOD
1. Pierce potatoes by using fork prongs.
2. Cover"
33104,2,"potatoes with waxed paper.  Heat on high until tender, about 5 to 10 minutes.

TO STUFF POTATOES:
1. Slice each potato in half, lengthwise.  Using a spoon, scoop out pulp, leaving about 1/4-inch thick shells, saving pulp.
2. Blend cheese, milk, and"
33104,3,"onion.  Add potato pulp; mix until light and fluffy.
3. Fill potato halves with mixture.  Sprinkle paprika over potatoes.

Note: Return to oven or microwave to reheat, for a few minutes, if desired."
